Result: 恶意软件代码更小、文档注释更少、每个函数的圈复杂度更高，类与闭包等抽象机制使用更少。漏洞分析显示恶意软件存在更多良性代码通常会避免的问题类型，表明恶意开发者在安全开发实践上投入极低。但整体代码质量指标与良性软件差异并不显著到足以完全区分。

Conclusion: 恶意软件的开发风格倾向于追求便捷性、操作隐秘性和规避能力，而非长期可维护性。将代码度量作为行为信号和策略选择的代理指标，定量软件分析能够丰富行为网络安全研究，为网络犯罪者的行为画像提供新视角和新方向。

Abstract: Malware research primarily studies the results, the methods, and the impact. Even from an offensive security perspective, what is examined is the method, not the development strategy of the offender. This study investigates the behavioral signatures and coding patterns embedded in the malware source code. By analyzing a large corpus of leaked malware code and comparing it with carefully selected benign open-source software, we apply static application security testing and compute multiple software metrics. Based on cognitive psychology and criminological theories, our work interprets differences in code structure and quality as behavioral indicators, reflecting distinct motivational structures, risk tolerances, and development strategies of malware authors compared to benign software developers. Our findings reveal that malware code is generally smaller, less documented, and exhibits higher cyclomatic complexity per function, with reduced use of abstraction mechanisms such as classes and closures. Vulnerability analysis further reveals that malware exhibits more issues of the types that benign code typically avoids, suggesting a minimal investment in secure development practices. These patterns imply a development style optimized for expedience, operational secrecy, and evasion rather than long-term maintainability. Nonetheless, the code quality metrics indicate that it does not deviate significantly from benign software enough to be distinctive. By framing code metrics as proxies for behavioral signals and strategic choices, we demonstrate how quantitative software analysis can enrich behavioral cybersecurity research, offering new insights into the practices and priorities of malware developers. Our results pave the way for further research in the behavioral profiling of cyber offenders.

</details>


### [341] [AttackPathGNN: Cross-function vulnerability detection in smart contracts using state interference graphs and conjunction pooling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05986)
*Gabriela Dobrita,Simona-Vasilica Oprea,Adela Bara*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出AttackPathGNN，一种将智能合约漏洞检测重构为显式攻击路径推理的图神经网络，通过状态干扰图和合取池化机制，在多个基准测试上达到92.3% F1分数，并能输出结构化修复报告。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于学习的Solidity智能合约检测器将漏洞检测降级为单函数内的语法模式匹配，但许多重大漏洞（如The DAO、Cream Finance）并非存在于单个函数中，而是函数间的关系及多种条件的组合导致了攻击可行。因此需要一种能捕获函数间交互关系的检测方法。

Method: 提出AttackPathGNN，包含两个核心设计：(1)状态干扰图——连接所有共享可变存储的函数对，包含类型化加权边和由五条件谓词定义的有向重入路径边；(2)合取池化——一种可微的AND聚合器，对八个命名的利用前提条件进行聚合，其log-sigmoid形式使得当任一缓解措施（重入锁、访问控制修饰符或SafeMath）到位时，每函数的利用分数就会归零。

Result: 在SmartBugs Wild测试集上达到92.3±0.2% F1分数，假阴性率4.3±0.3%；在独立人工标注的SmartBugs Curated基准上检测率达90.8±2.5%；在DASP10类别中6/10类别达到100%召回率，重入检测达98.7±1.8%。

Conclusion: AttackPathGNN能够有效检测跨函数的组合性漏洞，并且每个预测都附带结构化的修复报告，将检测结果转化为可操作、函数级别的审计发现，提升了漏洞检测的可解释性和实用性。

Abstract: Existing learning-based detectors for Solidity smart-contracts reduce vulnerability detection to syntactic pattern matching within single functions, yet many of the most consequential exploits (The DAO, Cream Finance) exist not in any individual function but in the relationship between functions and in the combination of conditions that made the attack feasible. Thus, we propose AttackPathGNN, a graph neural network (GNN) that reframes detection as reasoning over explicit attack paths. Two architectural choices distinguish it from prior GNN-based detectors: (1)a State Interference Graph that links every pair of functions sharing mutable storage through typed, weighted edges and through directed reentrancy-path edges defined by an explicit five-condition predicate; (2)conjunction pooling, a differentiable AND-aggregator over eight named exploit preconditions whose log-sigmoid form causes the per-function exploit score to collapse whenever any single mitigation (a reentrancy guard, an access-control modifier or SafeMath) is in place. Across five independent training runs, AttackPathGNN attains 92.3+/-0.2% F1 on the SmartBugs Wild held-out test partition (4.3+/-0.3% false-negative rate, 90.8+/-2.5% detection rate on the independently human-labelled SmartBugs Curated benchmark), recovering 6/10 DASP10 categories at 100% on every seed and Reentrancy at 98.7+/-1.8%. Each prediction is emitted with a structured remediation report, turning each verdict into an actionable, function-level audit finding.

It adopts a Vision-Language-Model (VLM)-based proposer to generate semantically targeted candidate edits and a Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) planner to prioritize promising edit paths while backtracking from ineffective ones. Together, the proposer and planner instantiate two key capabilities of human attackers, i.e., domain knowledge and iterative backtracking, respectively, to reproduce this practical threat. Our extensive experiments on UnsafeBench reveal profound systemic vulnerabilities: fewer than two edits on average enable 76.2% of unsafe images to evade detectors, while retaining 93.0% malicious semantics, meaning that such manipulated content remains perceptually malicious to humans while easily bypassing automated moderation. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究代码大语言模型在结构化剪枝压缩后是否仍能保留功能保持的代码突变能力，这一能力若在资源受限硬件上可部署，将带来严重安全威胁。

Method: 提出SecRL-Prune框架，对CodeLLM的前馈（MLP/FFN）通道进行结构化剪枝。从预训练教师模型出发，用强化学习学习逐层剪枝策略，以教师-学生KL散度为奖励。为提高效率，缓存教师模型top-P预测结果并与剪枝学生模型比较，避免同时占用GPU内存。

Result: 在HumanEval上对三个7B CodeLLM进行10-30%压缩，SecRL-Prune在pass@k和var@k指标上均优于近期结构化剪枝基线。真实恶意样本案例中，20%剪枝模型的语义保持突变显著减少了检测率。

Abstract: Large code language models (CodeLLMs) can generate and rewrite programs, enabling functionality-preserving code mutation that may be used to create diverse malware variants and evade signature-based detection. A key security question is whether this mutation capability survives model compression, which would make deployment feasible under limited hardware budgets. We propose SecRL-Prune, a structured pruning framework for CodeLLMs that operates on feed-forward (MLP/FFN) channels. Starting from a pretrained teacher, it learns a layer-wise pruning policy with reinforcement learning using a teacher-student KL-divergence reward. To improve efficiency, we cache the teacher's top-P predictions once and compare the pruned student against this compact target, avoiding simultaneous teacher-student residency in GPU memory. We evaluate SecRL-Prune on HumanEval using pass@k for execution correctness and var@k for code diversity across three 7B CodeLLMs at 10-30% compression. SecRL-Prune consistently preserves higher pass@k and var@k than recent structured pruning baselines under aggressive pruning. In a case study on real malware samples, semantics-preserving mutations from 20%-pruned models substantially reduced detections. These results show that code mutation capability can survive significant structured pruning, highlighting the security relevance of compressed CodeLLMs.

Although existing defense mechanisms are effective in some settings, they often suffer from limited generalizability and do not systematically improve model robustness across diverse attack scenarios. To address these limitations, we introduce Robust Ensemble of Selectively Strengthened and Augmented Predictors (RESSAP), a novel framework that transforms a single classifier into an ensemble of robust classifiers. Each classifier in the ensemble is trained on a carefully selected subset of features, where feature selection is guided by a resilience metric that accounts for both feature importance and robustness. During inference, a random subset of these classifiers is used to make predictions, increasing unpredictability and improving resistance to adversarial manipulation. In addition, noise-based data augmentation is applied during training to strengthen decision boundaries and improve generalization. Our experimental results demonstrate that RESSAP significantly improves robustness against adversarial evasion attacks while maintaining strong accuracy on clean data. Overall, this model-agnostic framework provides a scalable and flexible defense strategy for enhancing the security of machine learning systems without requiring major changes to existing architectures.

### [349] [WebMCP Tool Surface Poisoning: Runtime Manipulation Attacks on LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06387)
*Lin-Fa Lee,Yi-Yu Chang,Chia-Mu Yu,Kuo-Hui Yeh*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文发现WebMCP协议中存在一种新的安全威胁——会话中工具注入（MSTI），攻击者可利用第三方脚本在活跃会话中注入恶意工具，具体分为工具劫持（Tool Hijacking）和工具框架（Tool Framing）两种类型，并提出了相应的缓解方向和安全设计建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: WebMCP协议允许网站直接向AI代理暴露工具，绕过了传统用户界面，引入了新的安全风险，尤其是第三方脚本参与时攻击面扩大，现有研究缺乏对这类威胁的系统性分析。

Method: 对MSTI威胁进行分类，区分为工具劫持（利用AbortSignal API或注册竞争条件修改工具集）和工具框架（通过元数据字段如名称、描述、readOnlyHint、inputSchema影响代理对工具角色的感知），并通过实现验证两种攻击的有效性。

Result: 实验证明工具劫持和工具框架均能成功破坏WebMCP的预期功能。

Conclusion: MSTI源于WebMCP独特的工具生命周期和结构化元数据，工具表面本身成为新兴的安全关注点；提出了绑定工具身份与来源、确保生命周期一致性、强制第三方工具数据边界以及维护工具注册和调用的可追溯日志等缓解方向。

Abstract: WebMCP is a newly emerging protocol that enables websites to expose tools directly to AI agents, bypassing traditional user interfaces and introducing new security risks. The dynamic exposure of agent-accessible tools in WebMCP expands the attack surface of web sessions, especially when third-party scripts are involved. In this study, we identify a new potential threat, termed Mid-Session Tool Injection (MSTI), in which attackers leverage third-party scripts to inject malicious tools during an active session. To better characterize this threat, we classify MSTI based on the stage and target of manipulation, distinguishing between Tool Hijacking and Tool Framing. Tool Hijacking modifies the set of tools visible to the agent through mechanisms such as the AbortSignal API or race conditions during tool registration. In contrast, Tool Framing influences the agent's perception of tool roles through metadata fields such as tool name, description, readOnlyHint, and inputSchema. Our implementation demonstrates that both Tool Hijacking and Tool Framing can successfully disrupt the intended functionality of WebMCP. Based on these results, we outline potential mitigation directions and provide security design recommendations for WebMCP, including binding tool identity to its origin, ensuring lifecycle consistency, enforcing data boundaries for third-party tools, and maintaining traceable logs of tool registration and invocation. These findings indicate that MSTI arises from WebMCP's unique tool lifecycle and structured metadata, making the tool surface itself an emerging security concern.

</details>


### [350] [Will the Agent Recuse Itself? Measuring LLM-Agent Compliance with In-Band Access-Deny Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06460)
*Thamilvendhan Munirathinam*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出Recuse Signal，一种轻量级的带内退避信号，让服务器通过现有协议通道（如SSH横幅、PostgreSQL NOTICE）要求连接的大语言模型代理自愿退出。实验表明，该信号能100%触发代理退避，但效果是协作性的——可通过操作员授权覆写。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主LLM代理持有真实凭证并操作基础设施，但缺乏标准机制告知代理哪些资源不可访问。现有访问控制要么允许进入，要么硬性拒绝，无法区分代理与其他客户端。

Method: 定义了Recuse Signal作为开放迷你标准，实现了SSH横幅/PAM钩子和PostgreSQL线协议代理两种零/低足迹适配器，在真实生产主机部署并设计受控实验，观察代理收到信号后的退避行为。

Result: 在SSH场景下（GPT-4o、GPT-4o-mini、Claude Code），有信号时代理100%退避，无信号控制组100%完成任务。且信号是协作性的：最强大的模型在操作员授权框架下会继续执行，其他代理仍遵守主机策略。

Conclusion: Recuse Signal是一种有效的协作管控机制，类似于机器人协议（robots.txt）的线上对等物，但并非安全边界。标准、适配器和实验工具已开源以供复现。

Abstract: As autonomous LLM agents increasingly hold real credentials and operate infrastructure without a human in the loop, operators have no standard way to tell an agent that a resource is off-limits. Access controls either let the agent in (it has valid credentials) or hard-fail it (indistinguishable from any other client). We propose a third mode: a lightweight, published in-band deny signal -- the Recuse Signal -- that a server emits over a protocol's existing channels (an SSH banner, a PostgreSQL NOTICE) asking a connecting automated agent to voluntarily withdraw. This is a cooperative governance control, the robots.txt analogue for live access; it is explicitly not a security boundary. Its value is entirely empirical and, to our knowledge, unmeasured: do compliant LLM agents actually honor such a signal? We define the signal as an open mini-standard, implement two zero- or low-footprint adapters (an SSH banner/PAM hook and a PostgreSQL wire-protocol proxy), deploy them on a live production host, and run a controlled experiment in which fresh agents are given a benign operations task and observed for recusal. In a pilot (SSH; OpenAI GPT-4o and GPT-4o-mini; and Claude Code as a deployed agent), the signal cleanly induces recusal -- 100% recusal when present versus 100% task completion in a no-signal control -- and, revealingly, behaves as a cooperative rather than absolute signal: an explicit operator-authorization framing flips the most capable model to proceed, while other agents continue to defer to the on-host policy. We release the standard, adapters, and experiment harness for reproduction.

</details>

### [351] [RAINO: Anchoring Agents in Reality, A Systematic Review and Conceptual Framework for Realism in Agent-Based Modelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05167)
*Loïs Vanhée,Melania Borit*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文通过系统文献综述发现，基于Agent建模中的“现实主义”概念缺乏统一定义和框架，并提出了RAINO框架（现实锚点、输入、输出），用于系统化描述和论证模型中的现实主义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实主义是ABM的核心概念，但在文献中缺乏系统性的理论化和统一的操作化框架，导致概念模糊、方法选择缺乏合理解释。

Method: 采用系统文献综述方法，梳理当前ABM研究中如何操作化和证明现实主义，并基于综述结果构建RAINO框架。

Result: 现实主义定义模糊，缺乏一致的概念框架；实现和证明现实主义的方法多样，但缺乏方法适用性的充分解释。

Conclusion: RAINO框架通过区分现实锚点（经验数据、形式理论、专家知识、常识预期）及其在模型输入/输出中的应用，拓展了对现实主义的理解，解释了不同评估者对模型现实性评价差异的原因，并展示了不同框架视角对模型开发路径的影响。

Abstract: Realism is a central yet seemingly under-theorized concept in Agent-Based Modelling. This paper presents a Systematic Literature Review, aiming to identify how realism is currently operationalized and demonstrated. The results show that realism is often poorly defined and lacks a consistent conceptual framework. A wide variety of methods are used to achieve and demonstrate realism, but explanations of whether and why these methods are appropriate for their intended purposes are generally limited. Building on this review, we introduce the Reality Anchor, Input, Output (RAINO) framework. RAINO identifies the key structures used to argue for realism in Agent-Based Models, consisting of Reality Anchors (e.g., empirical data, formal theory, expert knowledge, common-sense expectations) and their application as model Input or Output. RAINO broadens existing perspectives on how realism is framed. It explains why different assessors may evaluate the realism of a model in different ways, and it shows how this broader framing can lead to significantly different approaches to model development.

</details>

Method: 利用LLM智能体动态选择并执行声明式交互协议，支持根据用户目标并发执行多个协议，无需专门训练。

Our contribution, Ahoy, addresses this question by creating LLM agents that dynamically select and enact declarative protocols to achieve user goals. We demonstrate that an \ahoy agent can correctly and intelligently enact multiple protocols - concurrently if appropriate to the user goal - without specialized training. Ahoy's significance lies in that it brings together declarative protocols and LLMs, both approaches that promise improved knowledge engineering for agents.

### [353] [Learning to Contest: Decentralized Robust Fairness in Cooperative MARL via Cross-Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06162)
*Can Savcı*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出CAN方法，通过置换等变交叉注意力策略推断自由骑手数量并做出相应响应，在分级资源竞争场景下实现了去中心化多智能体强化学习的公平性与鲁棒性平衡，接近集中式分配器的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公平合作MARL团队最大化平等福利时容易被自私智能体利用（搭便车问题），集中式的需求分配器虽可解决但剥夺了智能体自主权，去中心化策略是否鲁棒尚未解决。

Method: 提出CAN（Cross-Attention Network），一种置换等变交叉注意力策略，通过观测其他智能体的行为推断自由骑手数量并做出比例响应：无自由骑手时轮流合作，存在自由骑手时适度竞争。使用对抗联盟（PSRO）训练。

Result: CAN在分级竞争场景下保持低可剥削性（ρ≈1.2-1.5，未保护时ρ=N），效率接近集中式oracle（D=0时≈1.0，D≥1时0.83-0.96）。在另外两个游戏中表现出范围性而非通用性：多服务器游戏鲁棒性强，赢家通吃场景下失效。

Conclusion: 在分级资源竞争下，去中心化策略可以实现公平与鲁棒性的平衡，但存在适用边界：竞争杠杆强度决定鲁棒性程度，弱杠杆和大团队零样本迁移会降低性能。

Abstract: Fair cooperative multi-agent RL (MARL) teams maximizing egalitarian welfare are exploitable: a single selfish agent free-rides on the surplus fair agents forgo to raise the worst-off. A centralized need-based allocator removes it, but only by taking allocation out of agents' hands; whether decentralized policies can be robust was left open. We show this futility is an artifact of all-or-nothing contention. Under graded contention (a contested resource delivers $1-c$, wasting $c$), we prove that for any $c<1$ a worst-off cooperator that contests a free-rider strictly improves on yielding, so decentralized leverage exists (Prop. 1). Realizing it is a coordination problem under uncertainty: the number of free-riders is unknown and variable, so any fixed rule is dominated. We introduce CAN, a permutation-equivariant cross-attention policy over agents' observed behaviour that infers the number of free-riders and responds proportionally: turn-taking when none, contesting just enough when some. Trained against an adversarial league (PSRO), CAN keeps best-response exploitability low ($ρ\approx1.2$-$1.5$, vs. $ρ=N$ unprotected) across the contention range, wasting almost nothing at $D=0$ (efficiency $\approx1.0$) and retaining most of it at $D\geq1$ (efficiency 0.83-0.96), approaching the centralized oracle on both axes, no central allocator. Fair-MARL learners fail on complementary axes (GGF/FEN yield and are exploitable, SOTO all-contests and wastes), while CAN is both. On two further games we find clear scope, not blanket generality: CAN stays efficient and Pareto-dominates the fair learners, but its robustness holds only in proportion to the contest leverage: strong on a multi-server game, partial when it weakens, absent under winner-take-all (Prop. 1 fails). We also report its fragilities: weak leverage and zero-shot transfer to larger teams degrade it at high contention.

</details>


### [354] [A Swarm Approach to Public Transit Using On-demand Routing in a Slime-Mold-Inspired Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06189)
*Lindsay Burke,Maxfield Comstock,Jason Graham,Ruth Malenda,Simon Garnier,Petras Swissler*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于黏菌启发路由算法的分布式需求响应公交系统，通过动态路径规划和持续合作竞价机制实现乘客分配与动态换乘，在郊区、城市和半乡村场景中分别将乘客送达率提高28%、49%和101%，步行时间减少75%以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统需求响应公交系统存在运营成本高、可靠性低的问题，主要源于集中式手动调度方案的局限性。作者希望通过去中心化、动态路由的分布式系统来缓解这些问题。

Method: 采用黏菌启发式路由算法实现多车动态路径规划，引入动态换乘机制，通过公交车之间持续的合作竞价过程处理乘客分配和动态换乘。使用OpenStreetMap的真实地图网络在郊区、城市和半乡村场景中进行仿真实验。

Conclusion: 所提出的分布式黏菌启发式需求响应公交系统能够显著提升网络效率和乘客体验，有效解决传统DRT系统的高成本和低可靠性问题。

Abstract: Demand-responsive transit (DRT) is a flexible alternative to traditional, fixed-route mass-transit networks. Although DRT can function well in low-density communities, high operating costs and low reliability are common issues. We propose that these issues can be mitigated by moving from a centralized, manually-scheduled scheme to a distributed system capable of dynamically routing multiple vehicles using a slime-mold-inspired routing algorithm to maximize network effectiveness. We additionally introduce the method of dynamic transfers to further optimize transit network efficiency. All passenger allocation and dynamic transfers are handled via a continual cooperative bidding process by the buses. In this paper, we present simulated results for a swarm-driven transit network in suburban, urban, and semi-rural scenarios, using map networks pulled from OpenStreetMap. We show that our approach increases passenger delivery rates relative to a fixed-network approach by 28%, 49%, and 101%, respectively, and results in over 75% reduction in walking time in all cases.

### [355] [Where Do Large Language Models Fail on Competitive Programming? A Taxonomy of Failures by Algorithm Type and Difficulty Rating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05228)
*Ayush Kumar Jha,Shalini Jha*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了GPT-4o和Claude Sonnet 4.6在315道Codeforces编程题上的表现，发现CoT提示策略在算法推理任务中不仅无益反而有害：GPT-4o通过率从46.0%降至36.8%，Claude的编译错误增加244%。错误分析表明"错误答案"是主要失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM技术报告仅发布聚合通过率，掩盖了模型在特定算法领域的脆弱性。研究旨在揭示LLM在竞争性编程中的真实失败模式。

Method: 构建包含7类算法、3个难度级别的315道Codeforces问题平衡分类体系；在严格执行条件下控制温度(T=0.2)评估GPT-4o和Claude；通过消融实验对比直接零样本生成与零样本CoT的效果差异。

Result: CoT对GPT-4o有害（通过率从46.0%降至36.8%），加剧贪心逻辑弱点；Claude在CoT下逻辑基线较高（63.5%），但文本生成增加导致编译错误增加244%；"错误答案"是主要失败模式（GPT-4o超90%，Claude约70%）。

Conclusion: 标准提示工程技术无法弥合竞争性编程环境中的算法推理差距，CoT在算法推理任务中可能适得其反。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate increasing proficiency on competitive programming benchmarks, yet technical reports predominantly publish aggregate pass rates, obscuring domain-specific vulnerabilities. We present a systematic empirical study of LLM failure patterns using a balanced taxonomy of 315 Codeforces problems across seven algorithm categories and three difficulty tiers. We evaluate GPT-4o and Claude Sonnet 4.6 under strict execution-based conditions, controlling for temperature (T = 0.2). To isolate the impact of reasoning frameworks on algorithmic correctness, we conduct an ablation study comparing direct zero-shot generation against zero-shot Chain-of-Thought (CoT). Our findings reveal a severe divergence from standard NLP benchmarks: forcing CoT aggressively penalizes GPT-4o, dropping its pass rate from 46.0% to 36.8% and exacerbating a critical weakness in Greedy logic. Conversely, while Claude maintains a higher logical baseline (63.5% under CoT), the expanded text generation severely degrades its markdown instruction adherence, causing its Compile Errors to more than triple (from 9 to 31, a 244% increase). Furthermore, failure-mode analysis indicates that Wrong Answer (WA) is the dominant verdict for both models--accounting for over 90% of GPT-4o's and roughly 70% of Claude's unaccepted solutions. These findings empirically demonstrate that standard prompt engineering techniques fail to bridge the algorithmic reasoning gap in competitive programming environments.

### [356] [DeployBench: Benchmarking LLM Agents for Research Artifact Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05238)
*Yuanli Wang,Yaoyao Qian,Yue Zhang,Hanhan Zhou,Jindan Huang,Tianfu Fu,Qiuyang Mang,Huanzhi Mao,Wenhao Chai,Wendong Fan,Liqiang Jing*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: DeployBench是一个包含51个研究工件部署任务的跨领域基准测试（涵盖AI/ML、计算机系统和科学计算），评估了四个LLM代理，通过率仅为7.8%-51.0%，主要失败原因（97/154）是代理过早自我终止，未能完成论文指定的任务要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有环境设置基准无法覆盖研究工件部署的完整范围，包括多语言工具链、系统级依赖（如GPU/CUDA和内核配置）以及遗留工件的兼容性，这阻碍了LLM代理在真实科研环境中的自主部署能力。

Method: 构建了涵盖AI/ML、计算机系统和科学计算三个领域的51个研究工件部署任务基准DeployBench，每个任务通过隐藏管道执行论文指定实验并检查输出来验证。使用OpenHands评估了四个最先进的LLM。

Result: 四个LLM的通过率在7.8%到51.0%之间；154次失败中有97次是由于代理的完成判断问题（自我终止），代理的预完成检查验证的目标与论文指定的任务要求不匹配。

Conclusion: DeployBench揭示了当前LLM代理与自主部署能力之间的差距，并为科学研究代理提供了现实且具挑战性的测试平台。

Abstract: LLM agents have made rapid progress on software engineering and ML research tasks, but these advances often assume access to a working runnable environment. For research artifacts released alongside published papers, setting up such an environment from a fresh machine remains a major bottleneck. Existing environment setup benchmarks do not cover the full scope of research artifact deployment, which involves multi-language toolchains, system-level dependencies beyond containers (e.g. GPU/CUDA and kernel configurations), and legacy artifact compatibility. We introduce DeployBench, a multi-domain benchmark of 51 research-artifact deployment tasks spanning AI/ML, computer systems, and scientific computing, covering all these dimensions. Each task is verified by a hidden pipeline that executes the paper's designated experiment and checks its outputs. Evaluating four state-of-the-art LLMs with OpenHands yields pass-rates from 7.8% - 51.0% . Failures are dominated by a completion-judgment problem: 97 of 154 are agent-terminated self-stops, where the agent's pre-finish checks validate a different or weaker target than the paper-specific task requires. DeployBench highlights the gap between current agents and autonomous deployment, and offers a realistic testbed for scientific research agents.

Abstract: Building infrastructure-as-code (IaC) in cloud computing is a critical task, underpinning the reliability, scalability, and security of modern software systems. Despite the remarkable progress of large language models (LLMs) in software engineering -- demonstrated across many dedicated benchmarks -- their capabilities in developing IaC remain underexplored. Unlike existing IaC benchmarks that predominantly center on declarative paradigms such as Terraform and involve generating entire codebases from scratch, our benchmark reflects the incremental code edits common in enterprise development with imperative tools like the AWS CDK. We present SWE-InfraBench, a diverse evaluation dataset sourced from dozens of real-world IaC codebases that challenge LLMs to perform realistic code modifications in AWS CDK repositories. Each example requires models to implement changes to existing codebases based on natural language instructions, with success determined by passing provided test cases. These tasks demand sophisticated reasoning about cloud resource dependencies and implementation patterns beyond conventional code generation challenges. Our evaluation results reveal significant limitations in current LLMs showing that even state-of-the-art systems struggle with many tasks -- the best model, Sonnet 3.7, succeeds in only 34\% of cases, while specialized reasoning models like DeepSeek R1 achieve just 24% success. The SWE-InfraBench dataset is available at: https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/64e59070fd51c0278560b01eb5dc4f3c447d5268cdabe5a350d2969e4413fea5

### [358] [From Failed Trajectories to Reliable LLM Agents: Diagnosing and Repairing Harness Flaws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06324)
*Mengzhuo Chen,Junjie Wang,Zhe Liu,Yawen Wang,Qing Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: HarnessFix是一个迹引导的框架，通过将执行轨迹编译为中间表示（HTIR），归因故障到具体步骤和层，生成修复补丁，在多个基准上提升15.2%-50.0%的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自改进智能体和自动框架演化方法主要依赖最终结果进行优化，但无法诊断失败轨迹中的责任证据所在位置以及哪个框架层导致了不可靠行为，导致修改范围宽泛、间接或范围不当。

Method: HarnessFix将原始执行轨迹和框架代码编译为HTIR（归一化碎片化轨迹证据并捕获步骤级来源和控制流关系），归因故障到具体轨迹步骤和框架层，合并重复诊断为可操作的缺陷记录并映射到范围修复算子，最后生成并验证框架补丁。

Result: 在SWE-Bench Verified、Terminal-Bench 2.0 Verified、GAIA和AppWorld上，HarnessFix将初始框架的测试性能提升了15.2%-50.0%，优于人工设计和自我演化基线，并揭示了ETCLOVG层中反复出现的框架缺陷模式。

Conclusion: HarnessFix通过迹引导的故障诊断和框架修复方法，有效解决了现有方法无法准确定位故障证据和框架层的问题，显著提升了智能体框架的性能和可靠性。

Abstract: LLM-based agents increasingly rely on harnesses that provide execution environments, tool interfaces, context, lifecycle orchestration, observability, verification, and governance. Existing self-improving agents and automatic harness evolution methods mainly improve agents through runtime supervision, prompt optimization, workflow search, or harness modification based on final outcomes. However, they often fail to diagnose where the responsible evidence lies in failed trajectories and which harness layer causes the unreliable behavior, resulting in broad, indirect, or poorly scoped changes. This paper proposes HarnessFix, a trace-guided framework for diagnosing agent failures and repairing agent harnesses. HarnessFix compiles raw execution traces and harness code into a Harness-aware Trace Intermediate Representation (HTIR), which normalizes fragmented trajectory evidence and captures step-level provenance and control-flow relations. It then attributes failures to responsible trajectory steps and harness layers, consolidates recurring diagnoses into actionable flaw records, and maps them to scoped repair operators. Finally, HarnessFix generates and validates harness patches under flaw-specific repair specifications to reduce target flaws without introducing unacceptable regressions. We evaluate HarnessFix on SWE-Bench Verified, Terminal-Bench 2.0 Verified, GAIA and AppWorld. Across these benchmarks, HarnessFix improves held-out test performance over the initial harnesses by 15.2%--50.0%, outperforms human-designed and self-evolution baselines, and reveals recurring harness-flaw patterns across ETCLOVG layers.

</details>


### [359] [A Taxonomy of Runtime Faults in Model Context Protocol Servers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05339)
*Joshua Owotogbe,Indika Kumara,Willem-Jan van den Heuvel,Damian Andrew Tamburri,Antonio Ken Iannillo,Roberto Natella*

TL;DR: 本文首次对MCP（模型上下文协议）服务器运行时故障进行了实证分类，通过分析473个GitHub仓库中的837个故障线程，构建了包含11个顶层类别、27个子类别（73种叶级故障类型）的分类体系，并通过55名开发者调查验证了其外部有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP协议在工具增强型AI工作流中被广泛采用，但带来了配置参数被接受却未在运行时强制执行的可靠性挑战，这些运行时故障特征此前缺乏实证研究。

Method: 采用自底向上的开放式编码方法，手动分析了473个活跃维护的MCP服务器GitHub仓库中的837个MCP特定运行时故障线程，并通过55名MCP服务器开发者调查评估分类体系的外部有效性。

Result: 构建了包含11个顶层类别和27个子类别（73种叶级故障类型）的分类体系，涵盖协议交互、工具调用、模式强制、状态管理、模型-提供者集成、安全验证以及超时/显式取消等故障类别。受访开发者平均遇到20个子类别故障，无任何类别未被观察到。

Conclusion: 该分类体系反映了MCP系统中广泛观察到的运行时故障，将有助于未来AI软件的维护与演化。

Abstract: MCP (Model Context Protocol) enables LLMs (Large Language Models) to interact with external tools and data sources via a standardized protocol. Its rapid adoption in tool-augmented Artificial Intelligence (AI) workflows has introduced new reliability challenges, such as configuration parameters that are accepted but not enforced at runtime, leading to unintended default behavior, whose runtime fault characteristics remain empirically unexamined. We present the first empirical taxonomy of runtime faults in MCP servers. We manually analyzed 837 MCP-specific runtime fault threads from 473 actively maintained MCP server GitHub repositories and derived a taxonomy using a bottom-up open coding procedure. The taxonomy comprises 11 top-level categories and 27 subcategories (73 leaf fault types), covering recurrent failures across protocol interactions, tool invocations, schema enforcement, state management, model-provider integration, security validation, and timeouts or explicit cancellations of in-progress operations. To assess the taxonomy's external validity, we surveyed 55 MCP server developers. Respondents reported experiencing an average of 20 of the 27 fault subcategories, and no category remained unobserved. These results indicate that the taxonomy reflects widely observed runtime failures in MCP-based systems and shall assist AI software maintenance and evolution in the future.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对17位有经验的开发者进行半结构化访谈，采用探索性研究方法分析开发者的监督行为、挑战和策略。

Abstract: Autonomous software agents hold promise to increase developer productivity but make mistakes and exhibit novel failure modes, making human oversight central to successful human-agent collaboration. Existing research on agent oversight is largely conceptual; normative frameworks exist, but how users actually oversee agents is less known. In this paper, we bridge this gap by providing early empirical anchors for the theoretical discourse on agent oversight. Drawing on interviews with 17 experienced developers, we conduct an exploratory inquiry examining what forms of emergent oversight work developers perform, when, and how. We also document the oversight challenges developers face and the strategies they have started using to address them. We found at least four forms of emergent oversight work: a priori control, co-planning, real-time monitoring, and post hoc review. We show that oversight work is not only reactive and retrospective, as portrayed in existing research, but also preventative and proactive. We describe situated oversight challenges (e.g., difficulty reviewing agent-generated code) and outline heuristics developers adopt to address such challenges (e.g., using test results as guarantees for code correctness). We conclude with high-level takeaways, future research directions, implications for the human-centered design of software agents and for software engineering practice, and limitations of our research.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: RE讨论以实践和任务导向为主，重点关注调试、反编译和系统级分析；内存、固件和文件格式分析相关话题难度高且未解决率大。数据集还包含元数据和基于社区交互信号的难度指标。

The dataset comprises over 12,000 RE-related posts spanning more than 15 years. Using Latent Dirichlet Allocation (LDA) with Genetic Algorithm (GA)-based hyperparameter optimization, followed by manual topic labeling, we identify 23 semantically coherent RE topics grouped into six high-level thematic categories. The dataset is further enriched with metadata and difficulty indicators derived from community interaction signals, such as unanswered rates and response times.
  Our analysis reveals that RE discussions are predominantly practical and task-oriented, with strong emphasis on debugging, decompilation, and system-level analysis, while topics related to memory, firmware, and file format analysis exhibit high difficulty and unresolved rates. Beyond empirical characterization, REStack provides a reusable resource for empirical studies, educational research, and the development and evaluation of AI- and LLM-based developer assistance tools for RE. By releasing the dataset and accompanying scripts, this work aims to facilitate reproducible research and advance data-driven support for RE practice.

### [362] [ADK Arena: Evaluating Agent Development Kits via LLM-as-a-Developer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05548)
*Jintao Huang,Xiaomin Li,Gaurav Mittal,Yu Hu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出LLM-as-a-Developer方法论，通过构建ADK Arena自动化管道，系统评估了51个Python ADK框架在4个基准测试上的表现，发现框架选择对Agent性能有显著影响但无单一框架占优，生成成本差异达5.6倍，且不同信息源之间具有可替代性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Agent开发工具包（ADKs）快速涌现，但缺乏对其如何影响Agent性能的实证理解，需要一种可重复、可控的方法来评估不同框架的有效性和易用性。

Method: 提出LLM-as-a-Developer方法，用LLM编码Agent替代人类开发者学习框架API、编写并迭代修复代码；构建ADK Arena自动化管道，包含Docker隔离、三级验证流水线和多基准适配器，评估51个Python ADK框架。

Result: 57%的生成运行成功，成本跨框架变化5.6倍（0.6-3.4美元）；最佳ADK Agent解决高达80%的任务甚至超越通用前沿编码Agent，但中位数仅解决32%；信息源消融实验中，真实框架使用率在28-40%窄范围内。

Conclusion: 框架选择显著影响Agent性能但无单一最优框架；API复杂度（以成本衡量）并不直接预测成功；文档、源代码和参数知识在很大程度上可相互替代而非瓶颈。

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of Agent Development Kits (ADKs), SDK-level frameworks for building LLM-powered autonomous agents, has outpaced any empirical understanding of how framework choice affects agent performance. We propose \textbf{LLM-as-a-Developer}, a methodology that replaces human developers with an LLM coding agent that learns each framework's API from documentation, writes agent code, and iteratively repairs it through a validate-and-feedback loop until tests pass. By holding the developer constant and varying only the framework, generation effort becomes a quantitative proxy for API usability and the resulting agents provide a controlled measure of framework effectiveness. We implement this in \textbf{ADK Arena}, a fully automated pipeline with per-framework Docker isolation, a three-level validation pipeline, and benchmark adapters for SWE-bench, $τ^2$-bench, Terminal-Bench, and MCP-Atlas. Evaluating all 51 popular Python ADK frameworks (204 agent--benchmark pairs), we find that: (1)~generation succeeds for 57\% of runs, and its cost varies 5.6$\times$ across frameworks (\$0.6 to \$3.4 per agent), a quantitative proxy for API complexity, though cost alone does not predict success; (2)~no single framework dominates: the best single-benchmark ADK agents resolve up to 80\% of tasks and can even \emph{beat} general-purpose frontier coding agents at a fraction of the cost, yet the median framework resolves only 32\%; (3)~across information-source ablations, genuine framework usage stays within a narrow 28--40\% band (highest with raw source access and still 33\% with no reference material at all), indicating that documentation, source code, and parametric knowledge are largely substitutable rather than any one being a hard bottleneck.

This paper argues that the emergence of AI agents -- systems where large language models serve as the primary reasoning engine, dynamically generating and discarding code as an instrumental resource -- constitutes not an incremental improvement but a fundamental restructuring of the software paradigm. Drawing on first-principles analysis of complexity scaling, we formalize the distinction between traditional software (where code is the carrier of decision logic) and agentic systems (where code is ephemeral tooling for an LLM-driven reasoning loop). ### [365] [Enhancing Software Engineering Through Closed-Loop Memory Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05646)
*Xuehang Guo,Zora Zhiruo Wang,Qingyun Wang,Graham Neubig,Xingyao Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出MemOp闭环框架，将记忆效用建立在"验证过的下游影响"基础上，使其同时作为任务无关的评估基准和无注释的优化信号。通过单轮和跨轮记忆增强的互补评估来验证效果。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have enabled powerful software engineering (SE) agents capable of navigating complex codebases and resolving real-world issues. However, these agents remain fundamentally episodic: they fail to retain, refine, and reuse experiences across tasks, repeatedly reconstructing context from scratch and reproducing similar mistakes. Even with memory support, they offer no remedy for the absence of a principled, task-agnostic \textit{memory utility}, making them difficult to evaluate rigorously or generalize across agents and settings. To tackle these limitations, we introduce \ours, a closed-loop framework for memory augmentation in SE agents. \ours grounds memory utility in \textit{validated downstream impact}, establishing utility as both a task-agnostic \textbf{evaluation benchmark} and an annotation-free \textbf{optimization signal}. Through complementary evaluation on \textit{single-episode} and \textit{cross-episode} memory augmentation, results demonstrate that \ours consistently improves SE agents across settings, achieving absolute gains of up to $\uparrow5.25\%$ in success rate and $\uparrow4.63\%$ in resolve efficiency, while substantially reducing computational cost by $\geq9.79\%$.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用配对评估设置，将相同底层内容分别以干净英文和泰米尔语-英语代码混合形式表达，对比两者在阈值调优后的动作稳定性、审核负担变化以及误标率。

Abstract: Hate moderation is often evaluated as classification on clean English inputs, but deployed systems must route content to actions such as ALLOW, FLAG, or REVIEW. We study how this workflow changes under code-mixed inputs using a paired evaluation setting where the same underlying content is expressed as clean English and Tamil-English code-mix. Under thresholds tuned on clean English development data, code-mixed inputs produce substantial action instability, with a paired clean- to-code-mix decision flip rate of 0.265. The main workflow effects are increased review burden and increased false-flagging of non-hateful content: review rate rises from 0.138 to 0.297 and non-hate false-flag rate rises from 0.069 to 0.104. Tamil-only inputs show stronger degradation overall, suggesting a broader language-coverage limitation rather than the same code-mixed instability pattern. These results show that workflow-level evaluation reveals moderation failures that standard classification summaries can miss.

### [367] [Microskill Architecture: A Modular Skill-Driven Framework for AI-Native Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05720)
*Mohammad Zare,Omid Abdolrahmani*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出MicroSkill架构，一种受微服务启发的模块化设计范式，通过将知识封装为原子化技能胶囊并由动态路由器选择性调用，有效解决AI编码代理在大型项目中的上下文窗口管理问题。在15个复杂特性的企业内容管理系统案例中，该架构实现了90%以上的token消耗降低、近两倍的首次编译成功率提升，并完全消除了架构违规问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型和AI编码代理在软件开发中面临结构性挑战，尤其是上下文窗口管理问题：将完整项目文档和代码注入模型会导致中间信息丢失、token成本激增以及架构漂移。现有方法无法同时保证准确性和效率。

Method: 受微服务架构启发，将知识封装为原子化、边界清晰的技能胶囊（skill capsules），而非将服务分解；设计动态路由器（dynamic router），根据任务仅选择语义相关的胶囊；将上下文分配形式化为在token预算约束下的语义相关性最优化问题。

Result: 在包含15个复杂特性的企业内容管理系统案例中：token消耗降低超过90%；首次编译成功率几乎翻倍；完全消除了架构违规问题；通过自学习机制自主提取并注册了7个新的技能胶囊。

Conclusion: MicroSkill架构为构建AI原生开发系统提供了可扩展的基础，使系统更加高效、可靠，并具备随时间自我进化的能力。

Abstract: Large language models and AI coding agents have reshaped software development, but the path to fully AI-native systems faces structural challenges. Chief among them is managing context windows without losing accuracy or efficiency. When developers inject full project documentation and code into a model's memory, the model loses mid-sequence information, token costs spiral, and architecture drifts. This paper presents MicroSkill Architecture: a modular design paradigm inspired by microservices, applied to knowledge encapsulation instead of service decomposition. Instead of feeding an agent the entire codebase, the architecture partitions knowledge into atomic, sharply scoped skill capsules, and a dynamic router selects only semantically relevant capsules for the task. We formally model context allocation as constrained optimization over semantic relevance subject to a token budget. An empirical case study an enterprise content management system with fifteen complex features shows that MicroSkill cuts token consumption by over 90%, nearly doubles first-try compilation success rates, eliminates architectural violations entirely, and enables autonomous extraction and registration of seven new skill capsules via a self-learning mechanism. These findings suggest MicroSkill Architecture offers a scalable foundation for building AI-native development systems that are more efficient, more reliable, and capable of evolving over time.

</details>


### [368] [Human Oversight and Overload: Two Hidden and Costly Burdens of AI-Assisted Software Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05770)
*Vahid Garousi*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文揭示了AI辅助软件工程中两个常被忽视的负担：人类对AI生成物持续监督的需求，以及大量AI建议导致工程师认知过载的问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多聚焦AI提升效率的正面影响，忽略了AI工具给软件工程师带来的隐性负担和额外成本。

Method: 通过融合近期的从业者观点与实践证据，定性分析并总结AI辅助软件开发中的两类隐性负担。

Result: 识别出两个关键挑战：1) 人类必须持续审查、验证和重做AI产出；2) 大量AI建议导致开发者的认知负荷增加。

Conclusion: 呼吁软件工程团队正视并思考如何在日常AI辅助开发中应对这些隐性负担，开启相关讨论。

Abstract: AI is changing how software engineers work, but it often comes with hidden burdens and costs. In this paper, we characterize two such often-overlooked burdens: (1) the constant need for human oversight and inspection of AI-generated artifacts; and (2) the growing cognitive overload on software engineers from receiving large amounts of suggestions from AI tools. The need for human oversight is not optional-engineers must review, validate, and sometimes rework what AI produces. At the same time, the flood of AI suggestions, prompts, and possible solutions can leave developers mentally stretched. By blending evidence from recent opinions from practitioners, we highlight these often-overlooked challenges and open a conversation about how teams can handle them in day-to-day AI-assisted software engineering.

### [369] [Asuka-Bench: Benchmarking Code Agents on Underspecified User Intent and Multi-Round Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05920)
*Xin Wang,Liangtai Sun,Yaoming Zhu,Shuang Zhou,Jiaxing Liu,Fengjiao Chen,Lin Qiu,Xuezhi Cao,Xunliang Cai,Licheng Zhang,Zhendong Mao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: Asuka-Bench是一个面向Web开发的多轮交互式代码生成基准测试，包含50个任务、784条评估标准和2402个预期结果。它通过用户意图不明确的初始需求，结合多轮反馈闭环（代码代理→UI代理→用户LLM）来评估模型能力。实验显示模型间任务通过率差异达38个百分点，最强模型三轮后仅完成52%的项目，表明该基准远未饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码生成基准仅评估从完整提示到一次性输出的单一映射，而真实Web开发中用户很少一开始就写出完整规范，许多需求是在看到中间结果后才会明确。因此需要一个支持多轮细化的基准来评估模型在真实场景下的表现。

Method: 构建包含50个Web任务的基准，每个任务通过闭环解决：代码代理生成Web项目→UI代理在部署站点上执行测试→用户LLM将评估结果转化为自然语言反馈用于下一轮。共包含784条评估标准和2402个预期结果，在2个代理框架上评估8个LLM。

Result: 加权任务通过率在模型间差异达38个百分点，模型在从反馈中修复的能力上也存在显著差异。最强模型经过三轮后仅完成52%的项目，表明基准远未饱和。

Conclusion: Asuka-Bench有效区分了不同模型在多轮Web开发场景下的能力，揭示出现有模型在从用户反馈中迭代改进方面仍有很大提升空间。

Abstract: Existing code-generation benchmarks score a single mapping from a complete prompt to a one-shot output. However, real web development is different. Users seldom write a full spec at the start; many requirements only become clear once they look at an intermediate result and react to it. We present Asuka-Bench, a benchmark that pairs underspecified user intent with multi-round refinement, grounded in browser-rendered behavior. Each task is resolved through a closed loop: a Code Agent generates a web project, a UI Agent executes test cases on the deployed site, and a User LLM turns evaluation outcomes into natural-language feedback for the next round. The benchmark comprises 50 web tasks with 784 evaluation criteria and 2402 expected outcomes. We benchmark 8 LLMs across 2 agent frameworks. The results separate models clearly: weighted Task Pass Rate varies by 38 percentage points and models also differ substantially in their ability to repair from feedback. Asuka-Bench is also far from saturated: even the strongest model completes only 52% of projects after three rounds.

### [370] [Metamorphic Testing with the Rashomon Set: Explanation Faithfulness in Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06056)
*Helge Spieker,Jørn Eirik Betten,Arnaud Gotlieb*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 针对机器学习中的Rashomon效应（多个模型性能相近但解释不同），提出基于蜕变测试的框架，通过五个蜕变关系评估解释忠实性，无需真实标签即可验证特征归因的可信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习中存在Rashomon效应，即多个等效模型给出矛盾的特征解释，导致难以判断哪些解释可信。现有方法缺乏无真实标签情况下评估解释忠实性的手段。

Method: 提出基于蜕变测试的评估框架，定义五个蜕变关系来形式化模型行为与特征归因之间应具备的一致性属性，应用于SHAP和LIME两种事后解释方法，在两个表格回归数据集上验证。

Result: 该框架能有效评估解释方法的忠实性，在不依赖真实标签的前提下区分可靠与不可靠的解释，筛选出准确且解释可信的模型。

Conclusion: 该框架是一种实用、模型无关的工具，可用于选择具有可靠可解释性的高精度模型，填补了Rashomon效应下解释可信度评估的空白。

Abstract: Multiple machine learning models can achieve near-equivalent predictive performance on the same task, yet provide divergent feature-based explanations. This is called the Rashomon effect of (explainable) machine learning, and it raises the question of which explanations, if any, are trustworthy. We propose a framework based on metamorphic testing that assesses explanation faithfulness without requiring ground-truth labels by exploring attributed feature importance from post-hoc explanation methods. Five metamorphic relations formalize expected consistency properties between model behavior and feature attributions. We apply this general framework to two tabular regression datasets and two post-hoc explainers (SHAP and LIME) to demonstrate the approach. The framework offers a practical, model-agnostic tool for selecting accurate models with reliable and trustworthy explanations.

</details>


### [371] [TLA-Prover: Verifiable TLA+ Specification Synthesis via Preference-Optimized Low-Rank Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06133)
*Eric Spencer,Arslan Bisharat,Brian Ortiz,Khushboo Bhadauria,TaiNing Wang,George K. Thiruvathukal,Konstantin Laufer,Mohammed Abuhamad*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出TLA-Prover，一个200亿参数的模型，用于TLA+形式化规范合成。通过监督微调+基于修复的GRPO训练，在30个难题的测试集上达到30%的Gold和Diamond通过率，是未调优基线(8.6%)的3.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型生成的TLA+规范经常无法通过TLC模型检查器的语义验证，现有最好模型仅有26.6%的语法解析成功率和8.6%的语义模型检查通过率，亟需提升。

Method: 采用20B参数模型，先用已验证的示例进行监督微调(SFT)，再用基于修复的组相对策略优化(GRPO)训练。GRPO阶段模型学习修复自身被拒绝的规范，TLC直接提供奖励信号。设计了Bronze/ Silver/ Gold/ Diamond四级评估体系。

Result: TLA-Prover在30个难题基准上达到Gold和Diamond各30%的通过率（pass@1），是基线8.6%的3.5倍。DPO变体达到20% Diamond。Gold和Diamond在每个检查点一致，防止了平凡属性失败模式。

Conclusion: TLA-Prover显著提升了LLM生成TLA+规范的语义正确性，GRPO训练策略有效，且无需学习奖励模型，为形式化验证与LLM结合提供了有效路径。

Abstract: TLA+ is a formal specification language for verifying distributed systems and safety-critical protocols. Large language models (LLMs) frequently produce TLA+ specifications that fail the TLC model checker for semantic reasons. Across 25 LLMs, the best public baseline is 26.6% syntactic parse and 8.6% semantic model-check. We present TLA-Prover, a 20-billion-parameter model for TLA+ specification synthesis. Training combines supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on verified examples with repair-based group-relative policy optimization (GRPO). In the GRPO stage, the model learns to fix its own rejected specifications. We also train a direct preference optimization (DPO) variant from the same SFT checkpoint as an ablation. TLC provides the reward signal directly, with no learned reward model. Four tiers grade each output: Bronze (parses), Silver (no warnings), Gold (passes TLC), and Diamond. To reach Diamond, the model's correctness property is automatically altered in a small way; TLC must then detect a violation. If TLC still passes, the property was always-true and contributes nothing; the output fails Diamond. TLA-Prover reaches 9/30 (i.e. pass@1 = 30%) at both Gold and Diamond on a held-out 30-problem benchmark. This is roughly 3.5x the 8.6% untuned baseline. The DPO variant reaches 20% at Diamond. Gold and Diamond coincide at every checkpoint; this prevents the trivial-property failure mode.

Enhancing readability through targeted control is challenging due to its subjective nature. In this article, we employ representation engineering~(RepE) as the targeted control method given its characteristics of low data dependency and low computational cost. Prior work on RepE has primarily focused on the targeted control for a single task, but improving the code readability requires the control across multiple tasks. This study explores how problem domains and teaching methods influence motivation, engagement, inclusiveness, and feedback in modelling education. To investigate these dimensions, we conducted parallel surveys with 90 students and 22 educators. Our findings reveal disconnects between educator assumptions and student preferences: Students show greatest motivation for socially relevant domains and prefer choice in selection, while educators overestimate interest in study-related domains. The study identifies how minor design choices can exclude students. Students perceive feedback as meaningful when visibly acted upon. ### [374] [More than a Judge: An Empirical Study of Agent-Human Interaction in Crowdsourced Testing Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06301)
*Yue Wang,Yuan Zhao,Shengcheng Yu,Zhenyu Chen,Qing Gu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过受控人类实验（20名测试者，3个真实应用），研究了基于多智能体评估框架生成的反馈能否提升众包测试中的报告质量。结果表明，智能体反馈不仅能帮助测试者即时改进报告，还能迁移到后续任务中，验证了评估智能体从“事后评判者”转变为“流程中反馈提供者”的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有的多智能体评估框架（LLM-as-a-Judge）已被证明能减少评审负担并与人类共识高度一致，但该评估结果是否能实际改善测试者的工作表现尚不清楚。本文旨在填补这一空白，探究评估衍生的可操作反馈能否帮助测试者改进报告、提升后续任务表现并实现跨应用迁移。

Method: 采用四阶段受控人类实验，招募20名测试者在3个真实世界应用上进行众包测试。实验分为四个阶段：初始报告提交、收到智能体生成的评估反馈后修改、在新任务上进行首次提交（考察反馈迁移效果）、以及后续应用中的表现（考察跨应用迁移）。此外，17名参与者完成了事后问卷，补充定性反馈。

Result: 智能体生成的反馈支持了报告的即时改进；在接触反馈后的新任务中，测试者的首次提交质量有所提升；在后续应用任务中观察到部分但有意义的迁移效果。问卷结果进一步表明，反馈总体可理解、被用于修改，并延续到了后续任务中，但在反馈的具体性和执行层面仍存在改进空间。

Conclusion: 在众包测试场景下，评估智能体不仅可作为事后评判工具，还能作为工作流集成的反馈提供者，有效促进上游报告质量的提升。该研究为AI Agent在软件工程工作流中的落地提供了实证支持。

Abstract: Agentic AI is increasingly being integrated into software engineering workflows. In crowdsourced testing, however, the large volume and uneven quality of submitted reports still create a substantial review burden for developers. In prior work, we developed and validated a multi-agent assessment backbone based on the LLM-as-a-Judge paradigm. That backbone assesses reports along three dimensions--textuality, adequacy, and competitiveness--and was shown to align well with human consensus while substantially reducing assessment effort. Yet reliable automated judging does not by itself show whether agent outputs can improve human work when embedded into workflow. This paper studies that missing question in the context of crowdsourced testing. We investigate whether assessment-derived, actionable feedback can improve how testers revise reports, perform on later tasks, and transfer reporting practices across applications. To do so, we conducted a controlled four-stage human-subject study with 20 testers across three real-world applications. The results show that agent-generated feedback supports immediate improvements in revised reports, better first submissions on a new task after prior feedback exposure, and evidence of partial but meaningful transfer to a later application. A post-task questionnaire completed by 17 participants complements these artifact-based findings by suggesting that the feedback was generally understandable, acted upon in revision, and carried into later tasks, while also revealing remaining friction in specificity and execution. Overall, the study provides empirical evidence that, in the studied crowdsourced testing setting, assessment agents can serve not only as post-hoc judges but also as workflow-integrated feedback providers that support upstream report-quality improvement.

### [375] [Scaffold, Not Vocabulary? A Controlled, Two-Tier, Pre-Registered Study of a Popperian Code-Generation Skill](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06454)
*Mehmet Iscan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究发现，在代码生成任务中，波普尔式提示技能带来的性能提升主要源于提示的结构框架，而非其波普尔主义方法论内容本身。在大模型上所有条件均接近天花板无显著差异，在小模型上完整技能与仅保留标签的框架相比也无额外收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型越来越多地被用于编写、审查和评判代码，实践中常给模型配备提示"技能"要求其像科学家一样推理。波普尔式证伪主义提示被报告能改进生成代码，但这些收益几乎都通过LLM-as-a-judge评估，该工具存在已知的位置、自我偏好和风格偏见。研究者想知道：如果看似有用，收益是来自技能中的波普尔主义内容，还是来自任何提示框架所强加的结构？

Method: 采用两层级消融实验，设置三个对照组：长度匹配的安慰剂、仅保留波普尔标题但剥离过程步骤的标签框架、执行预言（HumanEval+单元测试）。还设置了词汇光环哨兵和同模型自评审计。在前沿模型Claude Sonnet 4.6和小模型Qwen2.5-Coder-0.5B上进行测试。

Result: 在前沿模型（N=163）上，所有条件均接近基准天花板，无显著差异，预注册的+5点改进未得到支持。在小模型（N=164）上，结构化提示使best-of-eight正确率提升20-22点，但完整技能相比仅标签框架无额外收益，安慰剂仅落后2.4点。0.5B模型使用波普尔评分标准进行自评时未优于随机选择，60%的选择集中在同一索引。

Conclusion: 在所测试的两个设置中，波普尔式程序性内容并未带来超越标签框架的额外执行正确性收益。收益来源于框架结构而非波普尔方法论内容本身。这是一个校准后的负结果，并提供了可复用的消歧协议。该发现限制了关于某一提示技能家族的工程主张，并非对波普尔方法论的总体评价。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly write, review, and judge code, and a fast-growing practice equips them with prompt 'skills' that ask the model to reason like a scientist. A prominent example tells the model to act as a Popperian falsificationist, and such skills are reported to improve generated code. But these gains are almost always read off an LLM-as-a-judge, an instrument with documented positional, self-preference, and stylistic biases. We ask: if it appears to help, is the gain from the skill's Popperian content, or from the structure any scaffold imposes? We pre-register a two-tier ablation with three controls: a length-matched placebo, a labels-only scaffold that keeps the Popperian headers but strips the procedure, and an execution oracle (HumanEval+ unit tests), plus a vocabulary-halo sentinel and a same-model self-judge audit. On a frontier model (Claude Sonnet 4.6, N=163) all conditions sit near the benchmark ceiling and do not separate, so the pre-registered +5-point improvement is not supported (a ceiling-limited non-detection). On a small model (Qwen2.5-Coder-0.5B, N=164) structured arms lift best-of-eight correctness by 20-22 points, but the full skill shows no separable benefit over a labels-only scaffold (aggregate F@8=L@8 vs V@8=34.8%), and the placebo trails by only 2.4 points. A 0.5B self-judge applying the Popperian rubric does not beat random selection and concentrates 60% of its picks on one index. In the two settings tested, the skill's Popperian procedural content adds no separable execution-correctness benefit beyond a labels-only scaffold, so the gains track scaffold structure. We contribute a calibrated negative result and a reusable disambiguation protocol; the finding bounds an engineering claim about one prompt-skill family and is not an evaluation of Popperian methodology in general.

</details>


### [376] [Code2LoRA: Hypernetwork-Generated Adapters for Code Language Models under Software Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06492)
*Liliana Hotsko,Yinxi Li,Yuntian Deng,Pengyu Nie*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出Code2LoRA框架，通过超网络为每个代码仓库生成专属LoRA适配器，在不增加推理token开销的情况下注入仓库级知识，支持静态和演化两种场景，在604个Python仓库基准上达到与逐仓库LoRA微调相当甚至更优的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码语言模型需要仓库级上下文来解决导入、API调用和项目约定问题。现有方法通过RAG检索或依赖分析注入长输入，或通过逐仓库微调和LoRA——但在仓库规模下成本高且对演化的代码库脆弱。

Method: 提出Code2LoRA框架，包含一个超网络（hypernetwork），为每个代码仓库生成专属LoRA适配器，实现零推理token开销的仓库知识注入。支持两种场景：Code2LoRA-Static（将单个仓库快照转换为适配器，适用于稳定代码库理解）和Code2LoRA-Evo（维护基于GRU隐藏状态的适配器，按代码diff更新，适用于演化中代码库）。同时构建RepoPeftBench基准，包含604个Python仓库的静态和演化两个赛道。

Result: 静态赛道：Code2LoRA-Static达到63.8%跨仓库和66.2%仓库内精确匹配，与逐仓库LoRA上限持平；演化赛道：Code2LoRA-Evo达到60.3%跨仓库精确匹配，比单一共享LoRA高出5.2个百分点。

Conclusion: Code2LoRA通过超网络生成仓库专属LoRA适配器，在不增加推理token开销的情况下有效注入仓库级知识，在静态和演化两种场景下均达到或超越现有方法，为代码语言模型的仓库级理解提供了高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Code language models need repository-level context to resolve imports, APIs, and project conventions. Existing methods inject this knowledge as long inputs (retrieved through RAG or dependency analysis) or through per-repository fine-tuning and LoRA -- costly at repository scale and brittle to evolving codebases. We introduce Code2LoRA, a hypernetwork framework that generates repository-specific LoRA adapters, effectively injecting repository knowledge with zero inference-time token overhead. Code2LoRA supports two usage scenarios: Code2LoRA-Static converts a single repository snapshot into an adapter, suitable for comprehension of stable codebases; while Code2LoRA-Evo maintains an adapter backed by a GRU hidden state updated per code diff, suitable for active development of evolving codebases. To evaluate Code2LoRA against parameter-efficient fine-tuning baselines, we build RepoPeftBench, a benchmark of 604 Python repositories with two tracks: a static track with 40K training and 12K test assertion-completion tasks, and an evolution track with 215K commit-derived training and 87K commit-derived test tasks. On the static track, Code2LoRA-Static achieves 63.8% cross-repo and 66.2% in-repo exact match, matching the per-repository LoRA upper bound; on the evolution track, Code2LoRA-Evo achieves 60.3% cross-repo exact match (+5.2 pp over a single shared LoRA). Code2LoRA's code can be found at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/code2lora-6857; the model checkpoints and RepoPeftBench datasets can be found at https://huggingface.co/code2lora.

</details>
